\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ A\ few\ intrinsics\ accept\ traditional\ data\ types\ like\ ints\ or\ floats,\ but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ most\ operate\ on\ data\ types\ that\ are\ specific\ to\ SSE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ a\ vector\ type\ ends\ in\ d,\ it\ contains\ doubles,\ and\ if\ it\ does\ not\ have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ a\ suffix,\ it\ contains\ floats.\ An\ integer\ vector\ type\ can\ contain\ any\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ integer,\ from\ chars\ to\ shorts\ to\ unsigned\ long\ longs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ int64x1\_t\ \_\_m64;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ float32x4\_t\ \_\_m128;\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ 128-\/bit\ vector\ containing\ 4\ floats\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ On\ ARM\ 32-\/bit\ architecture,\ the\ float64x2\_t\ is\ not\ supported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ data\ type\ \_\_m128d\ should\ be\ represented\ in\ a\ different\ way\ for\ related}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ intrinsic\ conversion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_\_aarch64\_\_)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00258\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ struct\ is\ defined\ in\ this\ header\ file\ called\ 'SIMDVec'\ which\ can\ be\ used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00259\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ by\ applications\ which\ attempt\ to\ access\ the\ contents\ of\ an\ \_m128\ struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00260\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ directly.\ \ It\ is\ important\ to\ note\ that\ accessing\ the\ \_\_m128\ struct\ directly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00261\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ bad\ coding\ practice\ by\ Microsoft:\ @see:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00262\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-\/us/library/ayeb3ayc.aspx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00263\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00264\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ However,\ some\ legacy\ source\ code\ may\ try\ to\ access\ the\ contents\ of\ an\ \_\_m128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00265\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ struct\ directly\ so\ the\ developer\ can\ use\ the\ SIMDVec\ as\ an\ alias\ for\ it.\ \ Any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00266\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ casting\ must\ be\ done\ manually\ by\ the\ developer,\ as\ you\ cannot\ cast\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00267\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ otherwise\ alias\ the\ base\ NEON\ data\ type\ for\ intrinsic\ operations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00268\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00269\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ union\ intended\ to\ allow\ direct\ access\ to\ an\ \_\_m128\ variable\ using\ the\ names}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00270\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ that\ the\ MSVC\ compiler\ provides.\ \ This\ union\ should\ really\ only\ be\ used\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00271\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ trying\ to\ access\ the\ members\ of\ the\ vector\ as\ integer\ values.\ \ GCC/clang}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00272\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ allow\ native\ access\ to\ the\ float\ members\ through\ a\ simple\ array\ access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00273\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ operator\ (in\ C\ since\ 4.6,\ in\ C++\ since\ 4.8).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00274\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00275\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Ideally\ direct\ accesses\ to\ SIMD\ vectors\ should\ not\ be\ used\ since\ it\ can\ cause}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00276\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\ performance\ hit.\ \ If\ it\ really\ is\ needed\ however,\ the\ original\ \_\_m128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00277\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ variable\ can\ be\ aliased\ with\ a\ pointer\ to\ this\ union\ and\ used\ to\ access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00278\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ individual\ components.\ \ The\ use\ of\ this\ union\ should\ be\ hidden\ behind\ a\ macro}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00279\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ that\ is\ used\ throughout\ the\ codebase\ to\ access\ the\ members\ instead\ of\ always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00280\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ declaring\ this\ type\ of\ variable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00281\ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{union\ }ALIGN\_STRUCT(16)\ SIMDVec\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{00315\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Function\ Naming\ Conventions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00316\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ naming\ convention\ of\ SSE\ intrinsics\ is\ straightforward.\ A\ generic\ SSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00317\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ intrinsic\ function\ is\ given\ as\ follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00318\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \_mm\_<name>\_<data\_type>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00319\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00320\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ parts\ of\ this\ format\ are\ given\ as\ follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00321\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 1.\ <name>\ describes\ the\ operation\ performed\ by\ the\ intrinsic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00322\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 2.\ <data\_type>\ identifies\ the\ data\ type\ of\ the\ function's\ primary\ arguments}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00323\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00324\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ last\ part,\ <data\_type>,\ is\ a\ little\ complicated.\ It\ identifies\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00325\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ content\ of\ the\ input\ values,\ and\ can\ be\ set\ to\ any\ of\ the\ following\ values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00326\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ +\ ps\ -\/\ vectors\ contain\ floats\ (ps\ stands\ for\ packed\ single-\/precision)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00327\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ +\ pd\ -\/\ vectors\ cantain\ doubles\ (pd\ stands\ for\ packed\ double-\/precision)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00328\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ +\ epi8/epi16/epi32/epi64\ -\/\ vectors\ contain\ 8-\/bit/16-\/bit/32-\/bit/64-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00329\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ signed\ integers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00330\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ +\ epu8/epu16/epu32/epu64\ -\/\ vectors\ contain\ 8-\/bit/16-\/bit/32-\/bit/64-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00331\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ unsigned\ integers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00332\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ +\ si128\ -\/\ unspecified\ 128-\/bit\ vector\ or\ 256-\/bit\ vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00333\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ +\ m128/m128i/m128d\ -\/\ identifies\ input\ vector\ types\ when\ they\ are\ different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00334\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ than\ the\ type\ of\ the\ returned\ vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00335\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00336\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ example,\ \_mm\_setzero\_ps.\ The\ \_mm\ implies\ that\ the\ function\ returns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00337\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ a\ 128-\/bit\ vector.\ The\ \_ps\ at\ the\ end\ implies\ that\ the\ argument\ vectors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00338\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ contain\ floats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00339\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00340\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ A\ complete\ example:\ Byte\ Shuffle\ -\/\ pshufb\ (\_mm\_shuffle\_epi8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00341\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ //\ Set\ packed\ 16-\/bit\ integers.\ 128\ bits,\ 8\ short,\ per\ 16\ bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00342\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \_\_m128i\ v\_in\ =\ \_mm\_setr\_epi16(1,\ 2,\ 3,\ 4,\ 5,\ 6,\ 7,\ 8);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00343\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ //\ Set\ packed\ 8-\/bit\ integers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00344\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ //\ 128\ bits,\ 16\ chars,\ per\ 8\ bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00345\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \_\_m128i\ v\_perm\ =\ \_mm\_setr\_epi8(1,\ 0,\ \ 2,\ \ 3,\ 8,\ 9,\ 10,\ 11,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00346\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 4,\ 5,\ 12,\ 13,\ 6,\ 7,\ 14,\ 15);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00347\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ //\ Shuffle\ packed\ 8-\/bit\ integers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00348\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \_\_m128i\ v\_out\ =\ \_mm\_shuffle\_epi8(v\_in,\ v\_perm);\ //\ pshufb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00349\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04271\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_\_aarch64\_\_)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04274\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04275\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ARMv7\ lacks\ vcgtq\_s64.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04276\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ is\ based\ off\ of\ Clang's\ SSE2\ polyfill:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04277\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (a\ >\ b)\ -\/>\ ((a\_hi\ >\ b\_hi)\ ||\ (a\_lo\ >\ b\_lo\ \&\&\ a\_hi\ ==\ b\_hi))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04278\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{04279\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Mask\ the\ sign\ bit\ out\ since\ we\ need\ a\ signed\ AND\ an\ unsigned\ comparison}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04280\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ it\ is\ ugly\ to\ try\ and\ split\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04281\ \ \ \ \ int32x4\_t\ mask\ =\ vreinterpretq\_s32\_s64(vdupq\_n\_s64(0x80000000ull));}
\DoxyCodeLine{04282\ \ \ \ \ int32x4\_t\ a\_mask\ =\ veorq\_s32(vreinterpretq\_s32\_m128i(a),\ mask);}
\DoxyCodeLine{04283\ \ \ \ \ int32x4\_t\ b\_mask\ =\ veorq\_s32(vreinterpretq\_s32\_m128i(b),\ mask);}
\DoxyCodeLine{04284\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Check\ if\ a\ >\ b}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04285\ \ \ \ \ int64x2\_t\ greater\ =\ vreinterpretq\_s64\_u32(vcgtq\_s32(a\_mask,\ b\_mask));}
\DoxyCodeLine{04286\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Copy\ upper\ mask\ to\ lower\ mask}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04287\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\_hi\ >\ b\_hi}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04288\ \ \ \ \ int64x2\_t\ gt\_hi\ =\ vshrq\_n\_s64(greater,\ 63);}
\DoxyCodeLine{04289\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Copy\ lower\ mask\ to\ upper\ mask}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04290\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\_lo\ >\ b\_lo}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04291\ \ \ \ \ int64x2\_t\ gt\_lo\ =\ vsliq\_n\_s64(greater,\ greater,\ 32);}
\DoxyCodeLine{04292\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Compare\ for\ equality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04293\ \ \ \ \ int64x2\_t\ equal\ =\ vreinterpretq\_s64\_u32(vceqq\_s32(a\_mask,\ b\_mask));}
\DoxyCodeLine{04294\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Copy\ upper\ mask\ to\ lower\ mask}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04295\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\_hi\ ==\ b\_hi}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04296\ \ \ \ \ int64x2\_t\ eq\_hi\ =\ vshrq\_n\_s64(equal,\ 63);}
\DoxyCodeLine{04297\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\_hi\ >\ b\_hi\ ||\ (a\_lo\ >\ b\_lo\ \&\&\ a\_hi\ ==\ b\_hi)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04298\ \ \ \ \ int64x2\_t\ ret\ =\ vorrq\_s64(gt\_hi,\ vandq\_s64(gt\_lo,\ eq\_hi));}
\DoxyCodeLine{04299\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ vreinterpretq\_m128i\_s64(ret);}
\DoxyCodeLine{04300\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04301\ \}}
